,"https://lh4.googleusercontent.com/-CiO2mfl6FHo/AAAAAAAAAAI/AAAAAAAAAXU/_1qp9F3viMY/photo.jpg",,"This is a cat we call Pirate. She is one of a feral colony that Ben has been feeding for a long time. She always hung back and wouldn't come to eat until he had moved away. One evening he was bent over putting down the food and he felt a tap on his back. Pirate (she didn't have a name then) was standing there with a very mangled eye. Ben got a carrier from his van and took her back to the PURR-FECT Thrift Store to spend the night. The next day he took her into the vet who said the eye couldn't be saved. The eye was removed, she was spayed, and she spent about two weeks with us in the PURR-FECT Thrift Store while she recovered. The interesting thing was, that even with all the trauma, she didn't become more afraid of people; instead, she actually became sort of affectionate.
